[Unit]
Description=SCALP Budget State Engine
After=network.target
Wants=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/scalp/project
ExecStart=/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/budget.py

Restart=always
RestartSec=2

KillSignal=SIGTERM
TimeoutStopSec=10
StandardOutput=append:/opt/scalp/project/logs/budget.stdout.log
StandardError=append:/opt/scalp/project/logs/budget.stderr.log

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

---- systemctl cat scalp-exec.service ----
# /etc/systemd/system/scalp-exec.service
[Unit]
Description=SCALP Exec Engine (FSM SAFE / IDEMPOTENT)
After=network.target
Wants=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
Group=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/scalp/project
ExecStart=/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/exec.py
Restart=always
RestartSec=2
KillSignal=SIGTERM
TimeoutStopSec=10

# Sécurité basique
NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

# /etc/systemd/system/scalp-mae-mfe.service
[Unit]
Description=SCALP - MFE / MAE Engine
After=network.target
Wants=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/scalp/project

ExecStart=/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/mae_mfe.py

Restart=always
RestartSec=2

# Sécurité / robustesse
KillSignal=SIGTERM
TimeoutStopSec=10

# Logs
StandardOutput=append:/opt/scalp/project/logs/mae_mfe.log
StandardError=append:/opt/scalp/project/logs/mae_mfe.err.log

# SQLite WAL friendly
Environment=PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

---- systemctl cat scalp-tunnel.service ----
# /etc/systemd/system/scalp-tunnel.service
[Unit]
Description=Scalp Cloudflare Named Tunnel
After=scalp-agent.service
Requires=scalp-agent.service

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
ExecStart=/usr/bin/cloudflared tunnel run scalp-agent
Restart=always
RestartSec=5
KillSignal=SIGTERM
TimeoutStopSec=10

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
